                    $objSearcherPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objSearchPath
                    $PrivilegedAccessManagement = $objSearcherPath.FindAll()
                    Remove-Variable SearchPath
                    $objSearchPath.Dispose()
                    $objSearcherPath.Dispose()
                }
                Catch
                {
                    Write-Warning ("{8}{1}{13}{9}{10}{4}{12}{3}{7}{6}{2}{11}{0}{14}{5}" -f 'ment F','DR',' Access ','l','ieving','e','ged','e','[Get-A','or','est] Error retr','Manage',' Privi','F','eatur')
                    Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                }
            }
        }
        Else
        {
            $ADDomain = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain()
            $ADForest = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetCurrentForest()

            # Get Tombstone Lifetime
            $ADForestTombstoneLifetime = ([ADSI]"LDAP://CN=Directory Service,CN=Windows NT,CN=Services,$($objDomainRootDSE.configurationNamingContext) ").tombstoneLifetime.value

            # Check Recycle Bin Feature Status
            If ([convert]::ToInt32($objDomainRootDSE.forestFunctionality,10) -ge 6)
            {
                $ADRecycleBin = ([ADSI]"LDAP://CN=Recycle Bin Feature,CN=Optional Features,CN=Directory Service,CN=Windows NT,CN=Services,CN=Configuration,$($objDomain.distinguishedName) ")
            }
            # Check Privileged Access Management Feature Status
            If ([convert]::ToInt32($objDomainRootDSE.forestFunctionality,10) -ge 7)
            {
                $PrivilegedAccessManagement = ([ADSI]"LDAP://CN=Privileged Access Management Feature,CN=Optional Features,CN=Directory Service,CN=Windows NT,CN=Services,CN=Configuration,$($objDomain.distinguishedName) ")
            }
        }

        If ($ADForest)
        {
            $ForestObj = @()

            # Values taken from https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/hh852281(v=wps.630).aspx
            $FLAD = @{
	            0 = ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'000','Win','dows2');
	            1 = ("{2}{0}{3}{1}" -f'dows2003/Int','rim','Win','e');
	            2 = ("{0}{2}{1}"-f'Windo','3','ws200');
	            3 = ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Wind','ows20','08');
	            4 = ("{1}{3}{0}{2}{4}" -f'0','W','8','indows20','R2');
	            5 = ("{0}{2}{1}{3}"-f'Win','ows20','d','12');
	            6 = ("{0}{3}{1}{2}" -f 'W','s20','12R2','indow');
                7 = ("{0}{1}{3}{2}" -f 'Win','do','s2016','w')
            }
            $ForestMode = $FLAD[[convert]::ToInt32($objDomainRootDSE.forestFunctionality,10)] + ("{0}{1}" -f'For','est')
            Remove-Variable FLAD

            $ObjValues = @(("{1}{0}" -f 'e','Nam'), $ADForest.Name, ("{0}{1}{3}{2}" -f 'Func','tio','vel','nal Le'), $ForestMode, ("{4}{2}{6}{5}{0}{1}{3}" -f'g ','Maste','N','r','Domain ','n','ami'), $ADForest.NamingRoleOwner, ("{4}{0}{1}{3}{2}" -f'hema ','M','ster','a','Sc'), $ADForest.SchemaRoleOwner, ("{2}{1}{0}" -f 'in','ootDoma','R'), $ADForest.RootDomain, ("{1}{2}{0}{3}"-f'o','Domain',' C','unt'), $ADForest.Domains.Count, ("{2}{1}{0}" -f 'nt','u','Site Co'), $ADForest.Sites.Count, ("{2}{0}{3}{1}" -f'o','t','Gl','bal Catalog Coun'), $ADForest.GlobalCatalogs.Count)

            For ($i = 0; $i -lt $($ObjValues.Count); $i++)
            {
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}{2}" -f'Cat','egor','y') -Value $ObjValues[$i]
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f 'lue','Va') -Value $ObjValues[$i+1]
                $i++
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ForestMode

            For($i=0; $i -lt $ADForest.Domains.Count; $i++)
            {
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}{2}" -f'ateg','C','ory') -Value ("{1}{2}{0}"-f'n','Dom','ai')
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f'lue','Va') -Value $ADForest.Domains[$i]
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }
            For($i=0; $i -lt $ADForest.Sites.Count; $i++)
            {
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{1}{0}"-f'ry','o','Categ') -Value ("{0}{1}"-f'Sit','e')
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f 'Valu','e') -Value $ADForest.Sites[$i]
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }
            For($i=0; $i -lt $ADForest.GlobalCatalogs.Count; $i++)
            {
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{1}{0}"-f'ry','ego','Cat') -Value ("{0}{3}{2}{4}{1}" -f 'Glo','og','alCata','b','l')
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f'e','Valu') -Value $ADForest.GlobalCatalogs[$i]
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }

            $Obj = New-Object PSObject
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}" -f 'Cat','gory','e') -Value ("{2}{4}{1}{3}{0}"-f 'me','ne','Tom',' Lifeti','bsto')
            If ($ADForestTombstoneLifetime)
            {
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f'Val','ue') -Value $ADForestTombstoneLifetime
                Remove-Variable ADForestTombstoneLifetime
            }
            Else
            {
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f'ue','Val') -Value ("{0}{1}{2}" -f'N','ot Retrie','ved')
            }
            $ForestObj += $Obj

            $Obj = New-Object PSObject
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f'Cate','gory') -Value (("{0}{4}{1}{5}{7}{3}{2}{6}"-f'R','Bi','r','2008 R2 onwa','ecycle ','n','ds)',' ('))
            If ($ADRecycleBin)
            {
                If ($ADRecycleBin.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'.Count -gt 0)
                {
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f 'Va','lue') -Value ("{1}{0}" -f'ed','Enabl')
                    $ForestObj += $Obj
                    For($i=0; $i -lt $($ADRecycleBin.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'.Count); $i++)
                    {
                        $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                        $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}"-f 'Categ','ry','o') -Value ("{2}{3}{1}{0}"-f'pe','ed Sco','En','abl')
                        $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f 'Va','lue') -Value $ADRecycleBin.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'[$i]
                        $ForestObj += $Obj
                    }
                }
                Else
                {
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f'V','alue') -Value ("{2}{1}{0}" -f 'd','isable','D')
                    $ForestObj += $Obj
                }
                Remove-Variable ADRecycleBin
            }
            Else
            {
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}"-f 'lue','Va') -Value ("{0}{1}" -f'Disa','bled')
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }

            $Obj = New-Object PSObject
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f 'C','ategory') -Value ("{2}{4}{7}{5}{3}{0}{6}{1}{8}"-f 't (2016','nw','Privil','anagemen','eged ','s M',' o','Acces','ards)')
            If ($PrivilegedAccessManagement)
            {
                If ($PrivilegedAccessManagement.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'.Count -gt 0)
                {
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}"-f'ue','Val') -Value ("{2}{1}{0}"-f 'd','ble','Ena')
                    $ForestObj += $Obj
                    For($i=0; $i -lt $($PrivilegedAccessManagement.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'.Count); $i++)
                    {
                        $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                        $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'y','Catego','r') -Value ("{2}{1}{0}"-f'abled Scope','n','E')
                        $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}"-f'e','Valu') -Value $PrivilegedAccessManagement.Properties.'msDS-EnabledFeatureBL'[$i]
                        $ForestObj += $Obj
                    }
                }
                Else
                {
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}"-f'lue','Va') -Value ("{0}{2}{1}" -f 'Disa','d','ble')
                    $ForestObj += $Obj
                }
                Remove-Variable PrivilegedAccessManagement
            }
            Else
            {
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f'Va','lue') -Value ("{0}{1}{2}" -f 'Dis','a','bled')
                $ForestObj += $Obj
            }

            Remove-Variable ADForest
        }
    }

    If ($ForestObj)
    {
        Return $ForestObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRTrust
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Trusts of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Trusts of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain
    )

    # Values taken from https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/cc223768.aspx
    $TDAD = @{
        0 = ("{0}{1}" -f 'Disa','bled');
        1 = ("{1}{0}" -f 'nbound','I');
        2 = ("{1}{0}"-f 'bound','Out');
        3 = ("{1}{2}{0}"-f 'nal','BiDire','ctio');
    }

    # Values taken from https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/cc223771.aspx
    $TTAD = @{
        1 = ("{0}{2}{1}"-f'Do','el','wnlev');
        2 = ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Up','leve','l');
        3 = "MIT";
        4 = "DCE";
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f 'A','DWS'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADTrusts = Get-ADObject -LDAPFilter (("{4}{3}{0}{1}{2}"-f 'ss=trus','t','edDomain)','jectCla','(ob')) -Properties DistinguishedName,trustPartner,trustdirection,trusttype,TrustAttributes,whenCreated,whenChanged
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{9}{11}{12}{15}{5}{13}{4}{6}{3}{7}{0}{1}{8}{2}{10}{14}{17}{16}"-f'umera','ti',' t',' e','hi','] Er','le','n','ng','[','rustedD','Get-ADRTru','s','ror w','oma','t','Objects','in ')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADTrusts)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Trusts: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADTrusts)) "
            # Trust Info
            $ADTrustObj = @()
            $ADTrusts | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{3}{0}{2}{1}" -f 'ourc','Domain','e ','S') -Value (Get-DNtoFQDN $_.DistinguishedName)
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'omain','Tar','get D') -Value $_.trustPartner
                $TrustDirection = [string] $TDAD[$_.trustdirection]
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{3}{1}{0}{2}"-f'i',' Direct','on','Trust') -Value $TrustDirection
                $TrustType = [string] $TTAD[$_.trusttype]
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}{2}" -f 'st ','Tru','Type') -Value $TrustType

                $TrustAttributes = $null
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000001) { $TrustAttributes += ("{3}{1}{0}{2}" -f 'sit',' Tran','ive,','Non') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000002) { $TrustAttributes += ("{0}{1}"-f'UpLev','el,') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000004) { $TrustAttributes += ("{3}{1}{0}{2}" -f'rantined','ua',',','Q') } #SID Filtering
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000008) { $TrustAttributes += ("{4}{3}{5}{0}{2}{1}" -f 'Tr','nsitive,','a','ores','F','t ') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000010) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{1}{5}{3}{6}{0}{4}" -f 'on','ss','Cro','rgani',',',' O','zati') } #Selective Auth
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000020) { $TrustAttributes += ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Wi','thin ','Forest,') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000040) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{1}{3}{4}{0}" -f'l,',' as','Treat',' Extern','a') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000080) { $TrustAttributes += ("{5}{2}{0}{1}{4}{3}"-f ' RC','4 Encr','s','ption,','y','Use') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000200) { $TrustAttributes += ("{1}{4}{2}{3}{0}" -f'tion,','N',' TGT',' Delega','o') }
                If ([int32] $_.TrustAttributes -band 0x00000400) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{0}{1}"-f 'IM ','Trust,','P') }
                If ($TrustAttributes)
                {
                    $TrustAttributes = $TrustAttributes.TrimEnd(",")
                }
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}" -f'Attri','es','but') -Value $TrustAttributes
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}{2}"-f'nC','whe','reated') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.whenCreated))
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{3}{2}{1}"-f'w','nged','ha','henC') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.whenChanged))
                $ADTrustObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADTrusts
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f'AP','LD'))
    {
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
        $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = ("{1}{2}{3}{0}{4}"-f'ed','(objectClas','s=t','rust','Domain)')
        $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{3}{2}{0}{4}{1}{5}" -f 'is','edna','u','disting','h','me'),("{2}{1}{3}{0}"-f'er','ustp','tr','artn'),("{3}{2}{1}{0}" -f'tion','rec','tdi','trus'),("{0}{3}{2}{1}"-f 'tr','type','st','u'),("{4}{2}{0}{3}{1}"-f 'ttribu','es','sta','t','tru'),("{2}{0}{1}"-f 'crea','ted','when'),("{3}{1}{0}{2}" -f 'nch','e','anged','wh')))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{0}{1}" -f 'Su','btree')

        Try
        {
            $ADTrusts = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{6}{10}{4}{0}{3}{7}{8}{1}{5}{9}{2}"-f 'r ','g trustedDo','ects','while e','Erro','m','[Get-','numera','tin','ain Obj','ADRTrust] ')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADTrusts)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Trusts: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADTrusts)) "
            # Trust Info
            $ADTrustObj = @()
            $ADTrusts | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}" -f 'So','n','urce Domai') -Value $(Get-DNtoFQDN ([string] $_.Properties.distinguishedname))
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{4}{1}{3}{2}{0}"-f 'n','t D','mai','o','Targe') -Value $([string] $_.Properties.trustpartner)
                $TrustDirection = [string] $TDAD[$_.Properties.trustdirection]
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{0}{1}"-f'Dire','ction','Trust ') -Value $TrustDirection
                $TrustType = [string] $TTAD[$_.Properties.trusttype]
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{1}{0}" -f 'e','t Typ','Trus') -Value $TrustType

                $TrustAttributes = $null
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000001) { $TrustAttributes += ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'ive,','No','n Transit') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000002) { $TrustAttributes += ("{1}{0}{2}"-f'el','UpLev',',') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000004) { $TrustAttributes += ("{3}{1}{2}{0}"-f 'ed,','nt','in','Quara') } #SID Filtering
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000008) { $TrustAttributes += ("{0}{4}{2}{3}{1}"-f'For','ive,','st Trans','it','e') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000010) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{3}{1}{0}" -f',','ion','Cross Org','anizat') } #Selective Auth
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000020) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{3}{0}{1}" -f'i','n Forest,','Wi','th') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000040) { $TrustAttributes += ("{1}{2}{0}{3}" -f 'as Ex','Treat',' ','ternal,') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000080) { $TrustAttributes += ("{2}{3}{0}{1}"-f 's RC','4 Encryption,','U','se') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000200) { $TrustAttributes += ("{0}{2}{3}{1}{4}" -f 'N','egat','o TGT ','Del','ion,') }
                If ([int32] $_.Properties.trustattributes[0] -band 0x00000400) { $TrustAttributes += ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'Trust,','PI','M ') }
                If ($TrustAttributes)
                {
                    $TrustAttributes = $TrustAttributes.TrimEnd(",")
                }
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}{2}" -f'ttribu','A','tes') -Value $TrustAttributes
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{3}{0}{2}{1}" -f 'Cr','ated','e','when') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whencreated))
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{1}{0}{3}"-f 'n','henCha','w','ged') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whenchanged))
                $ADTrustObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADTrusts
        }
    }

    If ($ADTrustObj)
    {
        Return $ADTrustObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRSite
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Sites of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Sites of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER objDomainRootDSE
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    RootDSE Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER DomainController
    [string]
    IP Address of the Domain Controller.

.PARAMETER Credential
    [Management.Automation.PSCredential]
    Credentials.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomainRootDSE,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [string] $DomainController,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [Management.Automation.PSCredential] $Credential = [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f'S','ADW'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $SearchPath = ("{0}{1}" -f'CN=S','ites')
            $ADSites = Get-ADObject -SearchBase "$SearchPath,$((Get-ADRootDSE).configurationNamingContext)" -LDAPFilter ("{0}{1}{3}{2}" -f '(objectCl','ass','te)','=si') -Properties Name,Description,whenCreated,whenChanged
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{0}{2}{6}{8}{3}{7}{1}{4}{5}"-f '[Get-ADRSite] ','te O','Error w','g S','bj','ects','hil','i','e enumeratin')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADSites)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Sites: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADSites)) "
            # Sites Info
            $ADSiteObj = @()
            $ADSites | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f'Nam','e') -Value $_.Name
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{1}{0}{3}" -f 'i','ipt','Descr','on') -Value $_.Description
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}"-f'ed','whenCr','eat') -Value $_.whenCreated
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}" -f'whe','d','nChange') -Value $_.whenChanged
                $ADSiteObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADSites
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}"-f'LDA','P'))
    {
        $SearchPath = ("{0}{1}{2}" -f 'CN=S','it','es')
        If ($Credential -ne [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty)
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$($DomainController)/$SearchPath,$($objDomainRootDSE.ConfigurationNamingContext)", $Credential.UserName,$Credential.GetNetworkCredential().Password
        }
        Else
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$SearchPath,$($objDomainRootDSE.ConfigurationNamingContext)"
        }
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objSearchPath
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = ("{2}{1}{0}{4}{3}"-f'a','objectCl','(','s=site)','s')
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{0}" -f 'btree','Su')

        Try
        {
            $ADSites = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{9}{7}{0}{3}{4}{6}{5}{11}{12}{10}{1}{8}{2}"-f 'ADRSite] ',' Site','jects','E','rror ','ile enu','wh','t-',' Ob','[Ge','ing','m','erat')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADSites)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Sites: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADSites)) "
            # Site Info
            $ADSiteObj = @()
            $ADSites | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f'Nam','e') -Value $([string] $_.Properties.name)
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}{3}{2}" -f 'Desc','rip','n','tio') -Value $([string] $_.Properties.description)
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}" -f 'ated','wh','enCre') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whencreated))
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{3}{1}{0}" -f 'd','ge','w','henChan') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whenchanged))
                $ADSiteObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADSites
        }
    }

    If ($ADSiteObj)
    {
        Return $ADSiteObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRSubnet
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Subnets of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Subnets of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER objDomainRootDSE
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    RootDSE Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER DomainController
    [string]
    IP Address of the Domain Controller.

.PARAMETER Credential
    [Management.Automation.PSCredential]
    Credentials.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomainRootDSE,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [string] $DomainController,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [Management.Automation.PSCredential] $Credential = [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}" -f'DWS','A'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $SearchPath = ("{0}{3}{1}{2}"-f 'CN=S',',CN','=Sites','ubnets')
            $ADSubnets = Get-ADObject -SearchBase "$SearchPath,$((Get-ADRootDSE).configurationNamingContext)" -LDAPFilter ("{2}{5}{4}{1}{0}{6}{3}"-f 'ub','s','(','et)','Class=','object','n') -Properties Name,Description,siteObject,whenCreated,whenChanged
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{7}{6}{1}{2}{0}{5}{9}{8}{4}{3}"-f'or while enu','bnet] E','rr','ects',' Obj','merat','RSu','[Get-AD','ng Subnet','i')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADSubnets)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Subnets: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADSubnets)) "
            # Subnets Info
            $ADSubnetObj = @()
            $ADSubnets | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f'ite','S') -Value $(($_.siteObject -Split ",")[0] -replace 'CN=','')
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f 'Nam','e') -Value $_.Name
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}{3}"-f 'Des','ripti','c','on') -Value $_.Description
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{0}{1}" -f 'te','d','whenCrea') -Value $_.whenCreated
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}" -f 'd','whenCha','nge') -Value $_.whenChanged
                $ADSubnetObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADSubnets
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}"-f 'LD','AP'))
    {
        $SearchPath = ("{3}{1}{0}{4}{2}"-f 'ts,','ubne','=Sites','CN=S','CN')
        If ($Credential -ne [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty)
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$($DomainController)/$SearchPath,$($objDomainRootDSE.ConfigurationNamingContext)", $Credential.UserName,$Credential.GetNetworkCredential().Password
        }
        Else
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$SearchPath,$($objDomainRootDSE.ConfigurationNamingContext)"
        }
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objSearchPath
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = ("{1}{3}{0}{2}" -f 'lass=subn','(','et)','objectC')
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{0}" -f 'ree','Subt')

        Try
        {
            $ADSubnets = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{3}{9}{12}{14}{11}{0}{10}{13}{2}{6}{8}{15}{7}{16}{5}{1}{4}"-f 'ub','jec',' ','[Ge','ts','ng Subnet Ob','E','ile enumer','rror w','t','net','S','-A',']','DR','h','ati')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADSubnets)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Subnets: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADSubnets)) "
            # Subnets Info
            $ADSubnetObj = @()
            $ADSubnets | ForEach-Object {
                # Create the object for each instance.
                $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}" -f'Sit','e') -Value $((([string] $_.Properties.siteobject) -Split ",")[0] -replace 'CN=','')
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f 'Na','me') -Value $([string] $_.Properties.name)
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{3}{1}{0}{2}"-f'criptio','s','n','De') -Value $([string] $_.Properties.description)
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{0}{3}{1}"-f 'Cr','d','when','eate') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whencreated))
                $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}{3}"-f'wh','an','enCh','ged') -Value ([DateTime] $($_.Properties.whenchanged))
                $ADSubnetObj += $Obj
            }
            Remove-Variable ADSubnets
        }
    }

    If ($ADSubnetObj)
    {
        Return $ADSubnetObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

# based on https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/heyscriptingguy/2012/01/05/how-to-find-active-directory-schema-update-history-by-using-powershell/
Function Get-ADRSchemaHistory
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Schema History of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Schema History of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER objDomainRootDSE
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    RootDSE Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER DomainController
    [string]
    IP Address of the Domain Controller.

.PARAMETER Credential
    [Management.Automation.PSCredential]
    Credentials.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomainRootDSE,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [string] $DomainController,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [Management.Automation.PSCredential] $Credential = [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}"-f'A','DWS'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADSchemaHistory = @( Get-ADObject -SearchBase ((Get-ADRootDSE).schemaNamingContext) -SearchScope OneLevel -Filter * -Property DistinguishedName, Name, ObjectClass, whenChanged, whenCreated )
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{9}{8}{3}{5}{7}{11}{1}{2}{0}{4}{6}{10}"-f'hile enumerating','ory] E','rror w','-ADRS',' Sc','che','he','m','et','[G','ma Objects','aHist')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADSchemaHistory)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Schema Objects: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADSchemaHistory)) "
            $ADSchemaObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::SchemaParser($ADSchemaHistory, $Threads)
            Remove-Variable ADSchemaHistory
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f 'DAP','L'))
    {
        If ($Credential -ne [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty)
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$($DomainController)/$($objDomainRootDSE.schemaNamingContext)", $Credential.UserName,$Credential.GetNetworkCredential().Password
        }
        Else
        {
            $objSearchPath = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry "LDAP://$($objDomainRootDSE.schemaNamingContext)"
        }
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objSearchPath
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = (("{2}{3}{4}{0}{1}"-f 'lass=','*)','(o','bj','ectC'))
        $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{3}{2}{0}{1}" -f'n','ame','tinguished','dis'),("{0}{1}" -f 'na','me'),("{2}{1}{3}{0}" -f'ss','bjectc','o','la'),("{3}{2}{0}{1}"-f 'ng','ed','ha','whenc'),("{2}{0}{1}{3}"-f'encr','eate','wh','d')))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'el','O','neLev')

        Try
        {
            $ADSchemaHistory = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{5}{2}{9}{13}{8}{7}{14}{6}{15}{1}{0}{10}{3}{11}{12}{4}"-f'e','e ','ADRSchemaHis','rat','cts','[Get-','r','E','y] ','t','nume','i','ng Schema Obje','or','rro',' whil')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADSchemaHistory)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Schema Objects: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADSchemaHistory)) "
            $ADSchemaObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::SchemaParser($ADSchemaHistory, $Threads)
            Remove-Variable ADSchemaHistory
        }
    }

    If ($ADSchemaObj)
    {
        Return $ADSchemaObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRDefaultPasswordPolicy
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Default Password Policy of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Default Password Policy of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f'AD','WS'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADpasspolicy = Get-ADDefaultDomainPasswordPolicy
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{15}{3}{14}{17}{13}{11}{7}{20}{8}{21}{1}{5}{2}{4}{19}{0}{9}{18}{6}{10}{12}{22}{16}" -f'umera',' ','rror wh','et','ile ','E','g the D','Pass','y','ti','efault P','ult','assword','RDefa','-','[G','icy','AD','n','en','wordPolic',']',' Pol')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADpasspolicy)
        {
            $ObjValues = @( ("{4}{0}{8}{2}{1}{7}{5}{3}{6}" -f'word h','ry','o','ord','Enforce pass','(passw','s)',' ','ist'), $ADpasspolicy.PasswordHistoryCount, "4", ("{0}{2}{3}{1}"-f 'R','5','eq.',' 8.2.'), "8", ("{0}{2}{4}{1}{3}" -f 'Con',' 04','tr','23','ol:'), ("{1}{2}{3}{0}" -f' more','24 ','o','r'),
            (("{5}{0}{2}{4}{3}{1}{7}{6}" -f 'm pas',' a','swo','d','r','Maximu','s)','ge (day')), $ADpasspolicy.MaxPasswordAge.days, "90", ("{2}{1}{0}"-f '. 8.2.4','eq','R'), "90", ("{3}{1}{4}{2}{0}" -f'23','rol:','4','Cont',' 0'), ("{0}{1}"-f '1 to',' 60'),
            (("{1}{2}{3}{7}{6}{4}{8}{0}{5}" -f'ys','Mini','m','um passwor','e ',')','g','d a','(da')), $ADpasspolicy.MinPasswordAge.days, "N/A", "-", "1", ("{4}{2}{3}{1}{0}"-f'23','4','n','trol: 0','Co'), ("{1}{0}"-f'r more','1 o'),
            (("{1}{0}{2}{5}{4}{3}" -f 'i','M','ni','haracters)','c','mum password length (')), $ADpasspolicy.MinPasswordLength, "7", ("{2}{0}{1}"-f'.',' 8.2.3','Req'), "13", ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Con','trol: 04','21'), ("{0}{1}{2}" -f '14 o','r m','ore'),
            ("{9}{10}{7}{0}{5}{4}{1}{6}{3}{2}{8}" -f ' ','ty ','e','m','omplexi','c','require','t','nts','Password m','ust mee'), $ADpasspolicy.ComplexityEnabled, $true, ("{2}{0}{1}" -f '. 8','.2.3','Req'), $true, ("{1}{2}{4}{0}{3}" -f 'l: 0','Co','n','421','tro'), $true,
            ("{12}{0}{8}{1}{6}{9}{5}{10}{3}{2}{7}{4}{11}" -f 'ore passw','u','ion f','pt',' in ',' e','s','or all users','ord ','ing reversible','ncry','the domain','St'), $ADpasspolicy.ReversibleEncryptionEnabled, "N/A", "-", "N/A", "-", $false,
            ("{0}{2}{6}{3}{4}{1}{5}"-f 'Acc','t','ount l','d','ura','ion (mins)','ockout '), $ADpasspolicy.LockoutDuration.minutes, (("{6}{3}{1}{2}{4}{0}{5}" -f 'r 3',' unl','ock) ','l','o','0','0 (manua')), ("{3}{2}{0}{1}" -f'8','.1.7','eq. ','R'), "N/A", "-", ("{2}{1}{0}"-f 'more',' or ','15'),
            ("{3}{4}{1}{5}{0}{2}" -f'mp','t lockout threshold (','ts)','A','ccoun','atte'), $ADpasspolicy.LockoutThreshold, ("{0}{1}"-f '1 to ','6'), ("{3}{0}{2}{1}" -f '.','6','1.','Req. 8'), ("{0}{1}"-f'1 t','o 5'), ("{2}{0}{1}{3}{4}" -f'ontro','l: ','C','1','403'), ("{0}{1}{2}" -f '1 t','o ','10'),
            ("{0}{6}{3}{1}{4}{2}{5}"-f 'Rese','o','after (m','t lock','ut counter ','ins)','t accoun'), $ADpasspolicy.LockoutObservationWindow.minutes, "N/A", "-", "N/A", "-", ("{2}{1}{0}"-f' more','r','15 o') )

            Remove-Variable ADpasspolicy
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f 'LD','AP'))
    {
        If ($ObjDomain)
        {
            #Value taken from https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/ms679431(v=vs.85).aspx
            $pwdProperties = @{
                ("{0}{2}{5}{1}{6}{4}{3}"-f 'DOM','SS','A','PLEX','_COM','IN_PA','WORD') = 1;
                ("{5}{3}{1}{2}{4}{0}{6}" -f 'N','N_PASSW','ORD_NO_A','I','NO','DOMA','_CHANGE') = 2;
                ("{4}{3}{0}{1}{8}{2}{7}{6}{5}"-f'N_PASSWORD','_NO_CL','A','OMAI','D','E','CHANG','R_','E') = 4;
                ("{1}{0}{2}{3}"-f 'OMAIN','D','_','LOCKOUT_ADMINS') = 8;
                ("{7}{2}{0}{6}{1}{5}{4}{3}" -f '_PASS','_','N','TEXT','R','STORE_CLEA','WORD','DOMAI') = 16;
                ("{6}{1}{4}{7}{3}{5}{0}{2}"-f'N','N_R','GE','AS','EFUS','SWORD_CHA','DOMAI','E_P') = 32
            }

            If (($ObjDomain.pwdproperties.value -band $pwdProperties[("{5}{4}{1}{3}{0}{2}{6}"-f 'MP','IN_PASSW','LE','ORD_CO','MA','DO','X')]) -eq $pwdProperties[("{1}{3}{0}{2}{4}"-f 'D_C','DOMAIN_PASSW','OMPLE','OR','X')])
            {
                $ComplexPasswords = $true
            }
            Else
            {
                $ComplexPasswords = $false
            }

            If (($ObjDomain.pwdproperties.value -band $pwdProperties[("{5}{8}{7}{0}{1}{4}{2}{3}{6}" -f 'SW','ORD_ST','_C','LEARTEX','ORE','DO','T','N_PAS','MAI')]) -eq $pwdProperties[("{1}{4}{2}{0}{5}{6}{3}"-f'P','DOM','N_','XT','AI','ASSWORD_STO','RE_CLEARTE')])
            {
                $ReversibleEncryption = $true
            }
            Else
            {
                $ReversibleEncryption = $false
            }

            $LockoutDuration = $($ObjDomain.ConvertLargeIntegerToInt64($ObjDomain.lockoutduration.value)/-600000000)

            If ($LockoutDuration -gt 99999)
            {
                $LockoutDuration = 0
            }

            $ObjValues = @( (("{1}{3}{2}{4}{5}{0}" -f 'rds)','En','orce password history (','f','passw','o')), $ObjDomain.PwdHistoryLength.value, "4", ("{3}{0}{1}{2}"-f ' 8.2','.','5','Req.'), "8", ("{3}{1}{2}{0}" -f '23','ntrol: 0','4','Co'), ("{1}{2}{0}"-f're','2','4 or mo'),
            ("{6}{4}{1}{0}{5}{8}{3}{7}{2}" -f'mum pass','i','(days)','age','x','w','Ma',' ','ord '), $($ObjDomain.ConvertLargeIntegerToInt64($ObjDomain.maxpwdage.value) /-864000000000), "90", ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Req.',' ','8.2.4'), "90", ("{1}{3}{2}{0}"-f '23','C','rol: 04','ont'), ("{0}{1}" -f '1 t','o 60'),
            ("{6}{2}{5}{7}{0}{3}{1}{4}" -f'rd age','days','s',' (',')','w','Minimum pas','o'), $($ObjDomain.ConvertLargeIntegerToInt64($ObjDomain.minpwdage.value) /-864000000000), "N/A", "-", "1", ("{2}{3}{0}{1}"-f' 04','23','Contro','l:'), ("{0}{1}"-f'1 ','or more'),
            (("{0}{5}{6}{10}{8}{9}{7}{3}{2}{4}{1}"-f'Mi','rs)','th (charact','word leng','e','ni','mu','s',' ','pas','m')), $ObjDomain.MinPwdLength.value, "7", ("{2}{0}{1}{3}"-f' 8','.2.','Req.','3'), "13", ("{1}{2}{0}" -f ': 0421','Cont','rol'), ("{3}{2}{0}{1}" -f'o','re','or m','14 '),
            ("{2}{3}{0}{5}{4}{1}{7}{6}"-f 'rd','mplexit','Pas','swo','co',' must meet ','uirements','y req'), $ComplexPasswords, $true, ("{2}{3}{1}{0}"-f'.2.3','8','Req','. '), $true, ("{2}{1}{0}{3}" -f '42','0','Control: ','1'), $true,
            ("{1}{7}{8}{3}{6}{10}{2}{0}{5}{4}{9}" -f'tion for all users i','Store','cryp','sword using reversi','e','n th','ble e',' p','as',' domain','n'), $ReversibleEncryption, "N/A", "-", "N/A", "-", $false,
            (("{5}{4}{0}{6}{7}{3}{1}{2}"-f'kout d','min','s)','(','ccount loc','A','ur','ation ')), $LockoutDuration, (("{5}{0}{2}{1}{4}{3}" -f'a','nl','l u','or 30','ock) ','0 (manu')), ("{0}{2}{1}" -f'Req. 8.1','7','.'), "N/A", "-", ("{2}{0}{1}" -f 'r mor','e','15 o'),
            (("{5}{7}{6}{4}{2}{3}{1}{0}" -f's)','pt','ld (atte','m','o','Account','kout thresh',' loc')), $ObjDomain.LockoutThreshold.value, ("{1}{0}{2}"-f ' ','1 to','6'), ("{2}{0}{1}" -f'.1.','6','Req. 8'), ("{1}{2}{0}" -f '5','1 t','o '), ("{1}{4}{0}{3}{2}" -f 'ol','Con','403',': 1','tr'), ("{2}{0}{1}" -f '1','0','1 to '),
            ("{6}{0}{4}{2}{5}{1}{3}"-f't loc','er (mi','out c','ns)','k','ounter aft','Reset accoun'), $($ObjDomain.ConvertLargeIntegerToInt64($ObjDomain.lockoutobservationWindow.value)/-600000000), "N/A", "-", "N/A", "-", ("{3}{2}{1}{0}"-f'more','or ','5 ','1') )

            Remove-Variable pwdProperties
            Remove-Variable ComplexPasswords
            Remove-Variable ReversibleEncryption
        }
    }

    If ($ObjValues)
    {
        $ADPassPolObj = @()
        For ($i = 0; $i -lt $($ObjValues.Count); $i++)
        {
            $Obj = New-Object PSObject
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{1}"-f 'P','licy','o') -Value $ObjValues[$i]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{2}{0}{1}" -f'ent',' Value','Curr') -Value $ObjValues[$i+1]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{3}{2}{1}" -f'PC','uirement','DSS Req','I ') -Value $ObjValues[$i+2]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{4}{2}{1}{3}" -f 'P','2.','v3.','1','CI DSS ') -Value $ObjValues[$i+3]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f 'SD ISM','A') -Value $ObjValues[$i+4]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{2}{3}{1}"-f'2018 ISM ','s','Con','trol') -Value $ObjValues[$i+5]
            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{5}{3}{4}{0}{2}" -f'ar','CI','k 2016','nch','m','S Be') -Value $ObjValues[$i+6]
            $i += 6
            $ADPassPolObj += $Obj
        }
        Remove-Variable ObjValues
        Return $ADPassPolObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRFineGrainedPasswordPolicy
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the Fine Grained Password Policy of the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the Fine Grained Password Policy of the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f'A','DWS'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADFinepasspolicy = Get-ADFineGrainedPasswordPolicy -Filter *
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{4}{3}{0}{6}{17}{14}{13}{8}{2}{9}{7}{5}{15}{12}{11}{16}{10}{1}"-f 'rai','y',' enumera','FineG','[Get-ADR','e Fine Gr','ned','th','hile','ting ','Polic','or','sw','w','ordPolicy] Error ','ained Pas','d ','Passw')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADFinepasspolicy)
        {
            $ADPassPolObj = @()

            $ADFinepasspolicy | ForEach-Object {
                For($i=0; $i -lt $($_.AppliesTo.Count); $i++)
                {
                    $AppliesTo = $AppliesTo + "," + $_.AppliesTo[$i]
                }
                If ($null -ne $AppliesTo)
                {
                    $AppliesTo = $AppliesTo.TrimStart(",")
                }
                $ObjValues = @(("{1}{0}"-f 'me','Na'), $($_.Name), ("{1}{0}{2}" -f 'es ','Appli','To'), $AppliesTo, ("{4}{2}{3}{0}{1}"-f'sswor','d history','rc','e pa','Enfo'), $_.PasswordHistoryCount, ("{5}{4}{2}{6}{3}{1}{0}{8}{7}"-f 'd ','swor','imum','s','ax','M',' pa','(days)','age '), $_.MaxPasswordAge.days, ("{1}{0}{3}{7}{4}{2}{6}{5}"-f 'mum p','Mini','ord ','a','w','(days)','age ','ss'), $_.MinPasswordAge.days, ("{0}{2}{1}{4}{3}"-f 'Minim','d l','um passwor','gth','en'), $_.MinPasswordLength, ("{5}{8}{6}{4}{2}{7}{0}{1}{3}" -f' require','ment','t com','s','ust mee','Pa',' m','plexity','ssword'), $_.ComplexityEnabled, ("{6}{4}{7}{1}{8}{5}{3}{9}{2}{0}"-f 'ncryption','us','e e','rsib',' password','e','Store',' ','ing rev','l'), $_.ReversibleEncryptionEnabled, ("{2}{4}{6}{3}{0}{5}{1}"-f'ation (m','ns)','Account','r',' lockout d','i','u'), $_.LockoutDuration.minutes, ("{2}{5}{1}{0}{4}{3}" -f'nt loc','u','Acc','old','kout thresh','o'), $_.LockoutThreshold, (("{5}{7}{0}{4}{2}{3}{6}{1}"-f ' loc','mins)','out coun','ter a','k','R','fter (','eset account')), $_.LockoutObservationWindow.minutes, ("{1}{2}{0}" -f 'ence','Pre','ced'), $($_.Precedence))
                For ($i = 0; $i -lt $($ObjValues.Count); $i++)
                {
                    $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{2}{0}" -f 'icy','P','ol') -Value $ObjValues[$i]
                    $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}"-f 'e','Valu') -Value $ObjValues[$i+1]
                    $i++
                    $ADPassPolObj += $Obj
                }
            }
            Remove-Variable ADFinepasspolicy
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f'LD','AP'))
    {
        If ($ObjDomain)
        {
            $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
            $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
            $ObjSearcher.Filter = (("{8}{5}{1}{3}{9}{0}{4}{2}{7}{10}{6}"-f'DS-Pas','ec','w','t','s','obj','ngs)','or','(','Class=ms','dSetti'))
            $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{0}{1}" -f 'Su','btree')
            Try
            {
                $ADFinepasspolicy = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{0}{10}{13}{12}{15}{4}{1}{8}{3}{14}{7}{17}{6}{2}{5}{16}{11}{9}"-f'[G','icy] Err','Gra',' while enumer','wordPol','in','e Fine ',' t','or','d Policy','et-ADRFineGraine','sswor','Pa','d','ating','ss','ed Pa','h')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }

            If ($ADFinepasspolicy)
            {
                If ([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADFinepasspolicy) -ge 1)
                {
                    $ADPassPolObj = @()
                    $ADFinepasspolicy | ForEach-Object {
                    For($i=0; $i -lt $($_.Properties.'msds-psoappliesto'.Count); $i++)
                    {
                        $AppliesTo = $AppliesTo + "," + $_.Properties.'msds-psoappliesto'[$i]
                    }
                    If ($null -ne $AppliesTo)
                    {
                        $AppliesTo = $AppliesTo.TrimStart(",")
                    }
                        $ObjValues = @(("{1}{0}"-f 'ame','N'), $($_.Properties.name), ("{2}{1}{0}{3}"-f 'ies T','l','App','o'), $AppliesTo, ("{0}{3}{1}{6}{4}{2}{5}"-f'E','c','word','nfor',' pass',' history','e'), $($_.Properties.'msds-passwordhistorylength'), ("{2}{5}{8}{4}{7}{0}{6}{3}{1}"-f 'wor','(days)','Maxi',' ','m pas','m','d age','s','u'), $($($_.Properties.'msds-maximumpasswordage') /-864000000000), ("{5}{3}{2}{1}{0}{4}" -f 'w','s','as','p','ord age (days)','Minimum '), $($($_.Properties.'msds-minimumpasswordage') /-864000000000), ("{4}{1}{2}{0}{3}" -f 'eng','um p','assword l','th','Minim'), $($_.Properties.'msds-minimumpasswordlength'), ("{0}{3}{8}{7}{5}{6}{4}{1}{2}" -f 'Pass','r','ements','word ','equi','t','y r','mplexi','must meet co'), $($_.Properties.'msds-passwordcomplexityenabled'), ("{3}{0}{2}{8}{6}{7}{4}{5}{1}"-f'ore password ','ption','u','St','i','ble encry','e','vers','sing r'), $($_.Properties.'msds-passwordreversibleencryptionenabled'), (("{3}{5}{8}{2}{7}{6}{4}{0}{1}"-f'ins',')','t ','Accoun',' (m','t lock','n','duratio','ou')), $($($_.Properties.'msds-lockoutduration')/-600000000), ("{5}{4}{2}{0}{1}{6}{3}" -f 'kout t','hres','nt loc','old','ccou','A','h'), $($_.Properties.'msds-lockoutthreshold'), (("{0}{5}{7}{8}{1}{3}{4}{6}{2}"-f 'Re','r','mins)',' aft','er','set account lockout co',' (','unt','e')), $($($_.Properties.'msds-lockoutobservationwindow')/-600000000), ("{1}{2}{0}{3}"-f 'nc','P','recede','e'), $($_.Properties.'msds-passwordsettingsprecedence'))
                        For ($i = 0; $i -lt $($ObjValues.Count); $i++)
                        {
                            $Obj = New-Object PSObject
                            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{0}{1}"-f'Polic','y') -Value $ObjValues[$i]
                            $Obj | Add-Member -MemberType NoteProperty -Name ("{1}{0}" -f 'alue','V') -Value $ObjValues[$i+1]
                            $i++
                            $ADPassPolObj += $Obj
                        }
                    }
                }
                Remove-Variable ADFinepasspolicy
            }
        }
    }

    If ($ADPassPolObj)
    {
        Return $ADPassPolObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRDomainController
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns the domain controllers for the current (or specified) forest.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns the domain controllers for the current (or specified) forest.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER Credential
    [Management.Automation.PSCredential]
    Credentials.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [Management.Automation.PSCredential] $Credential = [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f 'S','ADW'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADDomainControllers = @( Get-ADDomainController -Filter * )
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{13}{18}{7}{12}{9}{11}{15}{10}{3}{0}{1}{6}{4}{5}{16}{8}{14}{2}{17}"-f'u','m','oller','hile en','r','ati','e','RDo','g DomainC','ain','Error w','Con','m','[Get','ontr','troller] ','n',' Objects','-AD')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        # DC Info
        If ($ADDomainControllers)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Domain Controllers: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADDomainControllers)) "
            $DCObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::DomainControllerParser($ADDomainControllers, $Threads)
            Remove-Variable ADDomainControllers
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}" -f'DAP','L'))
    {
        If ($Credential -ne [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty)
        {
            $DomainFQDN = Get-DNtoFQDN($objDomain.distinguishedName)
            $DomainContext = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.DirectoryContext(("{0}{1}"-f'D','omain'),$($DomainFQDN),$($Credential.UserName),$($Credential.GetNetworkCredential().password))
            Try
            {
                $ADDomain = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetDomain($DomainContext)
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{9}{10}{8}{2}{12}{7}{0}{6}{4}{3}{5}{11}{1}"-f '] Er','xt','Co','mai','tting Do','n','ror ge','er','main','[Ge','t-ADRDo',' Conte','ntroll')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
            Remove-Variable DomainContext
        }
        Else
        {
            $ADDomain = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain()
        }

        If ($ADDomain.DomainControllers)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Domain Controllers: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADDomain.DomainControllers)) "
            $DCObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::DomainControllerParser($ADDomain.DomainControllers, $Threads)
            Remove-Variable ADDomain
        }
    }

    If ($DCObj)
    {
        Return $DCObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRUser
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns all users and/or service principal name (SPN) in the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns all users and/or  service principal name (SPN) in the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER date
    [DateTime]
    Date when ADRecon was executed.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER DormantTimeSpan
    [int]
    Timespan for Dormant accounts. Default 90 days.

.PARAMETER PageSize
    [int]
    The PageSize to set for the LDAP searcher object. Default 200.

.PARAMETER Threads
    [int]
    The number of threads to use during processing of objects. Default 10.

.PARAMETER ADRUsers
    [bool]

.PARAMETER ADRUserSPNs
    [bool]

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [DateTime] $date,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [int] $DormantTimeSpan = 90,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [int] $PageSize,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [int] $Threads = 10,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [int] $ADRUsers = $true,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [int] $ADRUserSPNs = $false
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f 'DWS','A'))
    {
        If (!$ADRUsers)
        {
            Try
            {
                $ADUsers = @( Get-ADObject -LDAPFilter ((("{8}{12}{1}{7}{14}{3}{13}{11}{9}{2}{6}{0}{10}{5}{4}" -f 'r','mA','vic','Type=8053','me=*))','alNa','eP','ccoun','(&(s','er','incip','s','a','06368)(','t'))) -ResultPageSize $PageSize -Properties Name,Description,memberOf,sAMAccountName,servicePrincipalName,primaryGroupID,pwdLastSet,userAccountControl )
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{9}{10}{11}{2}{1}{8}{6}{0}{12}{3}{7}{4}{5}" -f 'e','] ','ser','um','g UserSP','N Objects','whil','eratin','Error ','[','Ge','t-ADRU',' en')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
        }
        Else
        {
            Try
            {
                $ADUsers = @( Get-ADUser -Filter * -ResultPageSize $PageSize -Properties AccountExpirationDate,accountExpires,AccountNotDelegated,AdminCount,AllowReversiblePasswordEncryption,c,CannotChangePassword,CanonicalName,Company,Department,Description,DistinguishedName,DoesNotRequirePreAuth,Enabled,givenName,homeDirectory,Info,LastLogonDate,lastLogonTimestamp,LockedOut,LogonWorkstations,mail,Manager,memberOf,middleName,mobile,("{3}{1}{2}{0}{5}{4}" -f 'lowe','-','Al','msDS','gateTo','dToDele'),("{7}{1}{2}{4}{6}{0}{5}{3}"-f'pt','S-S','uppo','Types','rted','ion','Encry','msD'),Name,PasswordExpired,PasswordLastSet,PasswordNeverExpires,PasswordNotRequired,primaryGroupID,profilePath,pwdlastset,SamAccountName,ScriptPath,servicePrincipalName,SID,SIDHistory,SmartcardLogonRequired,sn,Title,TrustedForDelegation,TrustedToAuthForDelegation,UseDESKeyOnly,UserAccountControl,whenChanged,whenCreated )
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{7}{2}{8}{5}{10}{11}{1}{0}{4}{12}{9}{13}{14}{3}{6}"-f'il','ror wh','G','bje','e ','ADRUse','cts','[','et-','me','r] ','Er','enu','r','ating User O')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
        }
        If ($ADUsers)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Users: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADUsers)) "
            If ($ADRUsers)
            {
                Try
                {
                    $ADpasspolicy = Get-ADDefaultDomainPasswordPolicy
                    $PassMaxAge = $ADpasspolicy.MaxPasswordAge.days
                    Remove-Variable ADpasspolicy
                }
                Catch
                {
                    Write-Warning ("{15}{1}{2}{0}{4}{12}{16}{3}{13}{8}{14}{5}{7}{10}{9}{11}{6}"-f'r] Erro','Get-ADR','Use',' M','r retri','t Pass','s','word P','s','value a','olicy. Using ','s 90 day','ev','ax Pas','word Age from the Defaul','[','ing')
                    Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                    $PassMaxAge = 90
                }
                $UserObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::UserParser($ADUsers, $date, $DormantTimeSpan, $PassMaxAge, $Threads)
            }
            If ($ADRUserSPNs)
            {
                $UserSPNObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::UserSPNParser($ADUsers, $Threads)
            }
            Remove-Variable ADUsers
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f'AP','LD'))
    {
        If (!$ADRUsers)
        {
            $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
            $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
            $ObjSearcher.Filter = ((("{5}{14}{7}{9}{4}{2}{8}{11}{6}{0}{15}{3}{12}{13}{10}{1}" -f ')(servi','))','ype=','Princ','untT','(&(','306368','a','80','mAcco','me=*','5','ip','alNa','s','ce')))
            $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{0}{1}"-f'na','me'),("{2}{1}{3}{0}" -f 'n','rip','desc','tio'),("{1}{0}" -f'emberof','m'),("{2}{1}{0}"-f 'ountname','c','samac'),("{2}{4}{3}{1}{0}" -f'ame','aln','serv','ip','iceprinc'),("{4}{0}{2}{1}{3}" -f'ma','upi','rygro','d','pri'),("{2}{0}{1}" -f 't','set','pwdlas'),("{4}{3}{2}{1}{0}" -f 'ol','ontr','accountc','ser','u')))
            $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{0}{2}{1}" -f'S','ee','ubtr')
            Try
            {
                $ADUsers = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{9}{0}{5}{8}{4}{10}{6}{13}{11}{3}{1}{12}{7}{2}" -f 'Get-ADR','N ','ects','SP','r','U','le ','bj','ser] E','[','ror whi','numerating User','O','e')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
            $ObjSearcher.dispose()
        }
        Else
        {
            $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
            $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
            $ObjSearcher.Filter = ("{3}{0}{5}{1}{2}{4}" -f'mA','Typ','e=80530','(sa','6368)','ccount')
            # https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.directoryservices.securitymasks(v=vs.110).aspx
            $ObjSearcher.SecurityMasks = [System.DirectoryServices.SecurityMasks]("{0}{1}" -f'Dac','l')
            $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{2}{0}{1}"-f 't','Expires','accoun'),("{1}{2}{0}"-f 'ount','admin','c'),"c",("{2}{1}{0}" -f 'me','calna','canoni'),("{2}{1}{0}" -f'y','mpan','co'),("{0}{1}{2}" -f'depa','r','tment'),("{3}{2}{0}{1}" -f 'ipt','ion','escr','d'),("{0}{4}{2}{3}{5}{1}"-f 'dis','me','is','he','tingu','dna'),("{0}{1}{2}" -f 'g','ivenNam','e'),("{1}{0}{2}"-f'omedire','h','ctory'),("{0}{1}"-f 'i','nfo'),("{1}{3}{0}{2}"-f'm','la','estamp','stLogonti'),("{1}{0}" -f 'il','ma'),("{1}{0}{2}" -f'na','ma','ger'),("{0}{1}{2}" -f'm','em','berof'),("{2}{1}{0}"-f'e','am','middleN'),("{1}{0}{2}"-f 'ob','m','ile'),("{1}{2}{0}{3}{4}{5}"-f'ed','msD','S-Allow','ToD','el','egateTo'),("{2}{4}{5}{8}{3}{6}{1}{7}{0}"-f's','onTy','msDS','rt','-Su','pp','edEncrypti','pe','o'),("{1}{0}" -f 'e','nam'),("{4}{2}{3}{1}{0}" -f 'or','script','rity','de','ntsecu'),("{2}{1}{0}" -f'jectsid','b','o'),("{2}{0}{3}{4}{1}"-f 'ary','pid','prim','gro','u'),("{1}{0}{3}{2}" -f 'of','pr','lepath','i'),("{0}{2}{1}" -f'pwdL','stSet','a'),("{1}{2}{3}{0}"-f 'ountName','sa','m','acc'),("{2}{0}{1}" -f 'p','ath','script'),("{4}{3}{2}{1}{0}" -f'alname','p','nci','cepri','servi'),("{2}{1}{0}{3}" -f'ist','h','sid','ory'),"sn",("{1}{0}"-f'e','titl'),("{3}{1}{4}{0}{2}"-f 'ntro','oun','l','useracc','tco'),("{0}{2}{1}{4}{3}" -f'use','ta','rworks','ns','tio'),("{1}{0}{2}" -f 'ng','whencha','ed'),("{0}{2}{1}" -f 'when','ed','creat')))
            $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{0}{2}"-f 'r','Subt','ee')
            Try
            {
                $ADUsers = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{8}{7}{4}{2}{1}{6}{5}{3}{9}{0}"-f'User Objects','rr','E','era',' ','um','or while en',']','[Get-ADRUser','ting ')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
            $ObjSearcher.dispose()
        }
        If ($ADUsers)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Users: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADUsers)) "
            If ($ADRUsers)
            {
                $PassMaxAge = $($ObjDomain.ConvertLargeIntegerToInt64($ObjDomain.maxpwdage.value) /-864000000000)
                If (-Not $PassMaxAge)
                {
                    Write-Warning ("{0}{4}{17}{20}{1}{18}{5}{3}{8}{9}{14}{12}{10}{2}{19}{16}{6}{11}{15}{7}{13}"-f '[Get-ADRU','retrieving ','h','as','ser','ax P','ssword Pol','g value as 90 da','s','wor','e from t','ic','g','ys','d A','y. Usin','a','] ','M','e Default P','Error ')
                    Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                    $PassMaxAge = 90
                }
                $UserObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::UserParser($ADUsers, $date, $DormantTimeSpan, $PassMaxAge, $Threads)
            }
            If ($ADRUserSPNs)
            {
                $UserSPNObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::UserSPNParser($ADUsers, $Threads)
            }
            Remove-Variable ADUsers
        }
    }

    If ($UserObj)
    {
        Export-ADR -ADRObj $UserObj -ADROutputDir $ADROutputDir -OutputType $OutputType -ADRModuleName ("{1}{0}"-f's','User')
        Remove-Variable UserObj
    }
    If ($UserSPNObj)
    {
        Export-ADR -ADRObj $UserSPNObj -ADROutputDir $ADROutputDir -OutputType $OutputType -ADRModuleName ("{0}{2}{1}" -f 'U','s','serSPN')
        Remove-Variable UserSPNObj
    }
}

#TODO
Function Get-ADRPasswordAttributes
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns all objects with plaintext passwords in the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns all objects with plaintext passwords in the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER PageSize
    [int]
    The PageSize to set for the LDAP searcher object. Default 200.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.

.LINK
    https://www.ibm.com/support/knowledgecenter/en/ssw_aix_71/com.ibm.aix.security/ad_password_attribute_selection.htm
    https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/cc223248.aspx
    https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/cc223249.aspx
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [int] $PageSize
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}" -f'DWS','A'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADUsers = Get-ADObject -LDAPFilter ((("{4}{1}{7}{0}{9}{3}{8}{5}{6}{2}{10}"-f 'nixU','ssword=*','d=*','rPassword=*)(unicodePwd=*)(msSFU','({0}(UserPa','o','r',')(U','30Passw','se','))'))-f  [chAr]124) -ResultPageSize $PageSize -Properties *
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{15}{4}{5}{0}{9}{2}{1}{11}{7}{17}{8}{18}{16}{3}{13}{6}{10}{12}{14}"-f 'Pa','ordAttr','w','e enu','t-','ADR','g Pa','s] E','ror ','ss','ssw','ibute','ord Attr','meratin','ibutes','[Ge','il','r','wh')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADUsers)
        {
            Write-Warning "[*] Total PasswordAttribute Objects: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADUsers)) "
            $UserObj = $ADUsers
            Remove-Variable ADUsers
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}" -f'DAP','L'))
    {
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
        $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = (((("{11}{0}{5}{2}{6}{12}{8}{4}{10}{3}{1}{9}{7}"-f 'erP','P','s','SFU30','=*)(m','a','sword=*','))','ord=*)(unicodePwd','assword=*','s','({0}(Us',')(UnixUserPassw'))-f [chAr]124))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{0}{1}" -f 'Su','btree')
        Try
        {
            $ADUsers = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{7}{13}{5}{3}{4}{14}{0}{12}{9}{10}{1}{2}{6}{11}{15}{16}{8}" -f ' E','meratin','g','wordA','tt','et-ADRPass',' P','[','es','hil','e enu','a','rror w','G','ributes]','ss','word Attribut')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADUsers)
        {
            $cnt = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADUsers)
            If ($cnt -gt 0)
            {
                Write-Warning ('[*'+'] '+'Tot'+'al'+' '+'Pa'+'ssw'+'or'+'dAttri'+'bute '+'Objec'+'ts'+': '+"$cnt")
            }
            $UserObj = $ADUsers
            Remove-Variable ADUsers
        }
    }

    If ($UserObj)
    {
        Return $UserObj
    }
    Else
    {
        Return $null
    }
}

Function Get-ADRGroup
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns all groups and/or membership changes in the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns all groups and/or membership changes in the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER date
    [DateTime]
    Date when ADRecon was executed.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER PageSize
    [int]
    The PageSize to set for the LDAP searcher object. Default 200.

.PARAMETER Threads
    [int]
    The number of threads to use during processing of objects. Default 10.

.PARAMETER ADROutputDir
    [string]
    Path for ADRecon output folder.

.PARAMETER OutputType
    [array]
    Output Type.

.PARAMETER ADRGroups
    [bool]

.PARAMETER ADRGroupChanges
    [bool]

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [DateTime] $date,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [int] $PageSize,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [int] $Threads = 10,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $ADROutputDir,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [array] $OutputType,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [bool] $ADRGroups = $true,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [bool] $ADRGroupChanges = $false
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{1}{0}"-f'S','ADW'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADGroups = @( Get-ADGroup -Filter * -ResultPageSize $PageSize -Properties AdminCount,CanonicalName,DistinguishedName,Description,GroupCategory,GroupScope,SamAccountName,SID,SIDHistory,managedBy,("{5}{4}{3}{0}{6}{2}{1}"-f 'eMe','ata','aD','eplValu','sDS-R','m','t'),whenChanged,whenCreated )
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{2}{14}{0}{9}{5}{7}{13}{11}{8}{1}{3}{6}{4}{10}{12}"-f '] Er','a','[Get-','t','Group Obje','or w','ing ','hile','mer','r','c','nu','ts',' e','ADRGroup')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ($ADGroups)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Groups: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADGroups)) "
            If ($ADRGroups)
            {
                $GroupObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::GroupParser($ADGroups, $Threads)
            }
            If ($ADRGroupChanges)
            {
                $GroupChangesObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::GroupChangeParser($ADGroups, $date, $Threads)
            }
            Remove-Variable ADGroups
            Remove-Variable ADRGroups
            Remove-Variable ADRGroupChanges
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f'LD','AP'))
    {
        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
        $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = (("{4}{2}{1}{0}{3}" -f'oup','gr','objectClass=',')','('))
        $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{2}{1}{0}" -f'unt','dminco','a'),("{1}{2}{0}{3}" -f'ica','ca','non','lname'), ("{4}{2}{3}{0}{5}{1}" -f'ed','ame','ngu','ish','disti','n'), ("{2}{0}{1}"-f 'cript','ion','des'), ("{0}{1}{2}"-f'groupt','y','pe'),("{0}{1}{2}{3}"-f'sama','cc','ountn','ame'), ("{1}{3}{0}{2}"-f 't','s','ory','idhis'), ("{0}{2}{1}" -f'mana','edby','g'), ("{3}{2}{1}{5}{4}{0}" -f'ta','u','sds-replval','m','a','emetad'), ("{0}{1}{2}" -f'o','bje','ctsid'), ("{1}{0}{3}{2}" -f'he','w','ated','ncre'), ("{0}{2}{3}{1}" -f'w','nged','he','ncha')))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{0}"-f 'ee','Subtr')

        Try
        {
            $ADGroups = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{5}{4}{10}{6}{2}{3}{0}{1}{8}{7}{9}"-f 'um','erat','r whil','e en','up] E','[Get-ADRGro','o','g Group Object','in','s','rr')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ($ADGroups)
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total Groups: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADGroups)) "
            If ($ADRGroups)
            {
                $GroupObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::GroupParser($ADGroups, $Threads)
            }
            If ($ADRGroupChanges)
            {
                $GroupChangesObj = [ADRecon.LDAPClass]::GroupChangeParser($ADGroups, $date, $Threads)
            }
            Remove-Variable ADGroups
            Remove-Variable ADRGroups
            Remove-Variable ADRGroupChanges
        }
    }

    If ($GroupObj)
    {
        Export-ADR -ADRObj $GroupObj -ADROutputDir $ADROutputDir -OutputType $OutputType -ADRModuleName ("{0}{1}{2}"-f 'Gr','ou','ps')
        Remove-Variable GroupObj
    }

    If ($GroupChangesObj)
    {
        Export-ADR -ADRObj $GroupChangesObj -ADROutputDir $ADROutputDir -OutputType $OutputType -ADRModuleName ("{3}{2}{1}{0}" -f 'es','ang','h','GroupC')
        Remove-Variable GroupChangesObj
    }
}

Function Get-ADRGroupMember
{
<#
.SYNOPSIS
    Returns all groups and their members in the current (or specified) domain.

.DESCRIPTION
    Returns all groups and their members in the current (or specified) domain.

.PARAMETER Method
    [string]
    Which method to use; ADWS (default), LDAP.

.PARAMETER objDomain
    [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry]
    Domain Directory Entry object.

.PARAMETER PageSize
    [int]
    The PageSize to set for the LDAP searcher object. Default 200.

.PARAMETER Threads
    [int]
    The number of threads to use during processing of objects. Default 10.

.OUTPUTS
    PSObject.
#>
    param(
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [string] $Method,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry] $objDomain,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true)]
        [int] $PageSize,

        [Parameter(Mandatory = $false)]
        [int] $Threads = 10
    )

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}"-f 'ADW','S'))
    {
        Try
        {
            $ADDomain = Get-ADDomain
            $ADDomainSID = $ADDomain.DomainSID.Value
            Remove-Variable ADDomain
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{0}{7}{3}{6}{5}{2}{1}{8}{4}" -f'[Get','ing Domain C','t','up','text','ror get','Member] Er','-ADRGro','on')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        Try
        {
            $ADGroups = $ADGroups = @( Get-ADGroup -Filter * -ResultPageSize $PageSize -Properties SamAccountName,SID )
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{14}{2}{0}{5}{10}{7}{15}{16}{6}{1}{8}{4}{11}{13}{9}{12}{3}" -f 'A',' whi','Get-','p Objects',' enume','DRGroupMe','r','e','le',' G','mb','r','rou','ating','[','r','] Erro')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
        }

        Try
        {
            $ADGroupMembers = @( Get-ADObject -LDAPFilter ((("{1}{5}{2}{4}{7}{0}{6}{3}" -f'i','({0}(','be','))','ro','mem','d=*','f=*)(primarygroup')) -F  [cHaR]124) -Properties DistinguishedName,ObjectClass,memberof,primaryGroupID,sAMAccountName,samaccounttype )
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{12}{13}{15}{5}{4}{8}{0}{14}{1}{7}{2}{10}{6}{3}{9}{11}" -f' whi',' e','umerating G','Member','r','be','p','n','] Error',' Obje','rou','cts','[Ge','t','le','-ADRGroupMem')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }

        If ( ($ADDomainSID) -and ($ADGroups) -and ($ADGroupMembers) )
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total GroupMember Objects: $([ADRecon.ADWSClass]::ObjectCount($ADGroupMembers)) "
            $GroupMemberObj = [ADRecon.ADWSClass]::GroupMemberParser($ADGroups, $ADGroupMembers, $ADDomainSID, $Threads)
            Remove-Variable ADGroups
            Remove-Variable ADGroupMembers
            Remove-Variable ADDomainSID
        }
    }

    If ($Method -eq ("{0}{1}" -f 'LDA','P'))
    {

        If ($Credential -ne [Management.Automation.PSCredential]::Empty)
        {
            $DomainFQDN = Get-DNtoFQDN($objDomain.distinguishedName)
            $DomainContext = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.DirectoryContext(("{0}{1}"-f'Dom','ain'),$($DomainFQDN),$($Credential.UserName),$($Credential.GetNetworkCredential().password))
            Try
            {
                $ADDomain = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetDomain($DomainContext)
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{12}{1}{2}{13}{7}{3}{4}{6}{10}{5}{8}{11}{9}{0}" -f'xt','Get-ADRG','rou','er] Error ','gett','m','i','emb','a','e','ng Do','in Cont','[','pM')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                Return $null
            }
            Remove-Variable DomainContext
            Try
            {
                $ForestContext = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.DirectoryContext(("{1}{0}"-f'st','Fore'),$($ADDomain.Forest),$($Credential.UserName),$($Credential.GetNetworkCredential().password))
                $ADForest = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetForest($ForestContext)
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning ("{11}{0}{7}{2}{3}{8}{1}{12}{6}{9}{10}{4}{5}"-f'Ge','er]','-ADRGrou','p','ing For','est Context','r','t','Memb','or ge','tt','[',' Er')
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            }
            If ($ForestContext)
            {
                Remove-Variable ForestContext
            }
            If ($ADForest)
            {
                $GlobalCatalog = $ADForest.FindGlobalCatalog()
            }
            If ($GlobalCatalog)
            {
                $DN = "GC://$($GlobalCatalog.IPAddress)/$($objDomain.distinguishedname)"
                Try
                {
                    $ADObject = New-Object -TypeName System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry -ArgumentList ($($DN),$($Credential.UserName),$($Credential.GetNetworkCredential().password))
                    $ADDomainSID = New-Object System.Security.Principal.SecurityIdentifier($ADObject.objectSid[0], 0)
                    $ADObject.Dispose()
                }
                Catch
                {
                    Write-Warning "[Get-ADRGroupMember] Error retrieving Domain SID using the GlobalCatalog $($GlobalCatalog.IPAddress). Using SID from the ObjDomain. "
                    Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                    $ADDomainSID = New-Object System.Security.Principal.SecurityIdentifier($objDomain.objectSid[0], 0)
                }
            }
            Else
            {
                $ADDomainSID = New-Object System.Security.Principal.SecurityIdentifier($objDomain.objectSid[0], 0)
            }
        }
        Else
        {
            $ADDomain = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain()
            $ADForest = [System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetCurrentForest()
            Try
            {
                $GlobalCatalog = $ADForest.FindGlobalCatalog()
                $DN = "GC://$($GlobalCatalog)/$($objDomain.distinguishedname)"
                $ADObject = New-Object -TypeName System.DirectoryServices.DirectoryEntry -ArgumentList ($DN)
                $ADDomainSID = New-Object System.Security.Principal.SecurityIdentifier($ADObject.objectSid[0], 0)
                $ADObject.dispose()
            }
            Catch
            {
                Write-Warning "[Get-ADRGroupMember] Error retrieving Domain SID using the GlobalCatalog $($GlobalCatalog.IPAddress). Using SID from the ObjDomain. "
                Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
                $ADDomainSID = New-Object System.Security.Principal.SecurityIdentifier($objDomain.objectSid[0], 0)
            }
        }

        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
        $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = ("{1}{2}{3}{0}{4}" -f'ss=g','(obje','ctC','la','roup)')
        $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{0}{2}{3}{1}{4}" -f 'sam','co','a','c','untname'), ("{1}{2}{0}" -f'ctsid','o','bje')))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{0}{1}"-f 'Subtr','ee')

        Try
        {
            $ADGroups = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{4}{14}{10}{3}{5}{1}{7}{6}{11}{2}{9}{12}{8}{13}{0}"-f's','r wh','ra',' ','[Get-AD','Erro','le e','i','p','ti','er]','nume','ng Grou',' Object','RGroupMemb')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        $objSearcher = New-Object System.DirectoryServices.DirectorySearcher $objDomain
        $ObjSearcher.PageSize = $PageSize
        $ObjSearcher.Filter = ((("{2}{5}{1}{3}{4}{0}" -f 'marygroupid=*))','of','(n','=*)(','pri','IO(member')).rEplaCe('nIO','|'))
        $ObjSearcher.PropertiesToLoad.AddRange((("{0}{3}{1}{2}" -f'd','uishe','dname','isting'), ("{2}{0}{1}"-f 'nsho','stname','d'), ("{0}{2}{1}"-f 'obje','ss','ctcla'), ("{0}{3}{4}{2}{1}" -f 'prim','pid','u','arygr','o'), ("{0}{1}{2}" -f 'me','mber','of'), ("{2}{1}{0}"-f'tname','un','samacco'), ("{3}{1}{2}{0}"-f'pe','ac','countty','sam')))
        $ObjSearcher.SearchScope = ("{1}{2}{0}"-f 'e','S','ubtre')

        Try
        {
            $ADGroupMembers = $ObjSearcher.FindAll()
        }
        Catch
        {
            Write-Warning ("{8}{2}{14}{13}{11}{3}{7}{15}{4}{10}{5}{16}{1}{17}{9}{12}{0}{6}"-f 'ber O','ating Gr','Get-','be','r','ile enume','bjects','r]','[','upM','or wh','em','em','roupM','ADRG',' Er','r','o')
            Write-Verbose "[EXCEPTION] $($_.Exception.Message) "
            Return $null
        }
        $ObjSearcher.dispose()

        If ( ($ADDomainSID) -and ($ADGroups) -and ($ADGroupMembers) )
        {
            Write-Verbose "[*] Total GroupMember Objects: $([ADRecon.LDAPClass]::ObjectCount($ADGroupMembers)) "
